        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1312564460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7687737872010720663">I already knew I liked Zink's writing style from the few stand alone books of her's I tried so when in the mood for something different in YA, I decided it was high time I tried her series. A series about things I don't normally like to read about, but that I'm still inexplicably drawn to. <br/><br/>So off for a good time I went with little trepidation and a whole lot of expectation. <br/><br/>With a setting in the late 19th century this was quite the surprise and one I was thrilled with, I happen to love this era </span>
  <span id="freeText7687737872010720663" style="display:none">I already knew I liked Zink's writing style from the few stand alone books of her's I tried so when in the mood for something different in YA, I decided it was high time I tried her series. A series about things I don't normally like to read about, but that I'm still inexplicably drawn to. <br /><br />So off for a good time I went with little trepidation and a whole lot of expectation. <br /><br />With a setting in the late 19th century this was quite the surprise and one I was thrilled with, I happen to love this era for many reasons and jump at the chance to read anything involving it. <br /><br /> I devoured this. I loved it, couldn't get enough of it, and was oddly fascinated with it. <br /><br />The clues behind the prophecy, the two sisters, the other girls, the tragedies, the very prominent supernatural element to the storyline, all of it. </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer350861241625503368">I have been dying to read this book, and I finally got my hands on a copy! I've heard so much about it, but the book itself is 10 times better than what anyone can say. The plot will keep you on the edge of your seat, and you'll feel as though you've been holding your breath through some parts. With it's unexpected ending, 3 dimensional characters, enticing plot, and beautiful writing, Zink gives you a story no one could forget.</span>

          </span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer46859036" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5410231976595125005">This is an amazing story about two sisters on different paths with twists and turns that come at unexpected times. A very fast read with a lot of symbolism both sutbtle and dark. I enjoyed it very much and can't wait to see what happens next.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/775972.Spellbound"><img alt="Spellbound (Sweep, #6)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1503518268l/775972._SY160_.jpg" />

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3W8ntavGr5yxfZ7bZ/JGjiwT8GgdbcM39I+rVCPUkC9RvUEYU+E45WdNbmMGeasr7cnbmk2FTl5t9sH1bugN3g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RzMVUIc6qkDPcc2ro94ogjkMeGcAi+amAwpiYbzOQjzL4XP9fx09ORlBPRPCVcUn+NZTlVBja8+acwjA8fLfzQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
